# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the CSI driver integration: the CSI node plugin client, the CSI volume attach/detach controller, the CSI volume provisioner, and the PersistentVolume controller that bridges CSI operations to the core storage API.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the org domain.

- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

I've created a comprehensive `answer.json` file containing **14 core files** and **31 key symbols** that implement the Kubernetes CSI driver integration:

### Key Components Found:

1. **CSI Node Plugin Client** (2 files):
   - `csi_plugin.go` - Main plugin implementation and registration handler
   - `csi_client.go` - gRPC-based client for node operations (NodeGetInfo, NodePublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, etc.)

2. **CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller** (2 files):
   - `csi_attacher.go` - Implements volume attach/detach via VolumeAttachment objects
   - `attach_detach_controller.go` - Orchestrates attachment lifecycle and CSI node management

3. **CSI Volume Provisioner** (2 files):
   - `pv_controller.go` - Handles dynamic provisioning and CSI migration
   - `pv_controller_base.go` - Initializes CSI translator and migration manager

4. **CSI Node Integration** (3 files):
   - `csi_mounter.go` - Handles mount/unmount operations (SetUpAt/TearDownAt)
   - `csi_block.go` - Block device staging and publishing
   - `nodeinfomanager.go` - Maintains CSI node information and topology

5. **Supporting Components** (5 files):
   - `csi_drivers_store.go` - Registry of active CSI drivers
   - `csi_node_updater.go` - Manages CSINode allocatable updates
   - `expander.go` - Volume expansion support
   - `csi_util.go` - Utility functions
   - `csi_metrics.go` - Volume metrics provider

The answer file includes detailed symbols and a comprehensive narrative explaining how these components integrate to provide CSI driver support in Kubernetes.

It manages CSI driver registration through the RegistrationHandler interface and coordinates with the volume plugin manager.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_client.go`: Defines the csiClient interface which abstracts all node-level CSI operations including NodeGetInfo, NodePublishVolume, NodeStageVolume, NodeUnpublishVolume, NodeUnstageVolume, and NodeExpandVolume. This interface communicates with CSI drivers via gRPC.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_drivers_store.go`: Maintains a thread-safe store of registered CSI drivers with their endpoints and supported versions.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller\\n\\nThe **CSI volume attach/detach controller** implementation includes:\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_attacher.go`: The csiAttacher struct implements both the volume.Attacher and volume.Detacher interfaces. It handles volume attachment by creating VolumeAttachment objects and detachment by updating their status. The Attach and Detach methods orchestrate communication with CSI drivers through gRPC.\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/attachdetach/attach_detach_controller.go`: The main attach/detach controller that manages the lifecycle of volume attachments. It maintains desired and actual state of world, uses the attacherDetacher OperationExecutor to perform operations, and integrates with CSI through CSINodeLister for topology-aware scheduling.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Provisioner\\n\\nThe **CSI volume provisioner** is integrated into:\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller.go`: The PersistentVolumeController handles dynamic provisioning by creating external provisioner requests and includes support for CSI migration from in-tree plugins. The provisionClaimOperationExternal method routes provisioning requests to the appropriate CSI driver based on StorageClass configuration.\\n- `pkg/controller/volume/persistentvolume/pv_controller_base.go`: Provides the base controller setup, initializes the CSI translator for in-tree plugin migration, and manages the CSI migration manager.\\n\\n## CSI Node Integration\\n\\nThe CSI node integration for volume operations includes:\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_mounter.go`: The csiMountMgr struct implements mount/unmount operations. SetUpAt performs node staging and publishing, while TearDownAt handles unpublishing and unstaging of volumes.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_block.go`: The csiBlockMapper handles block device operations through SetUpDevice (NodeStageVolume) and TearDownDevice (NodeUnstageVolume), managing device staging and publishing for block volumes.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go`: The nodeInfoManager maintains CSI node information including driver node IDs, topology keys, and allocatable resources. The UpdateCSIDriver method updates the CSINode object with driver-specific information.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_node_updater.go`: The csiNodeUpdater watches CSIDriver objects and manages per-driver goroutines that periodically update CSINodeDriver allocatable information.\\n\\n## CSI Volume Expansion\\n\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/expander.go`: Implements NodeExpand for online volume expansion by querying driver capabilities and calling the CSI NodeExpandVolume RPC.\\n\\n## Supporting Utilities\\n\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_util.go`: Provides utility functions for credential management, volume data persistence, and secret handling.\\n- `pkg/volume/csi/csi_metrics.go`: Implements the MetricsProvider interface for reporting volume metrics like capacity and usage.\\n\\n## Integration Flow\\n\\nThe CSI driver integration works as follows: When a CSI driver registers, the RegistrationHandler validates it and stores it in DriversStore. For volume operations, the attach/detach controller uses the csiAttacher to create VolumeAttachment objects, triggering external-attacher components. The PersistentVolumeController orchestrates provisioning by identifying CSI-based StorageClasses and creating provision requests. On nodes, the csiMountMgr and csiBlockMapper implement mount/unmount and device setup operations using the csiClient. Node information is managed by nodeInfoManager which updates CSINode objects with topology and capacity information. The CSI translator enables seamless migration from in-tree storage plugins to CSI drivers by translating volume specifications and routing operations appropriately.\"\n}\n",
